This is a sample report, created with celerystalk to demonstrate the project. The scanned hosts in this report are all retired Hackthebox.eu machines.
This report was generated with the following commands:
CommandNotes
./celerystalk workspace create -w htb -o /assessments/htb -m vapt Create a named workspace, and specify output directory and mode
./celerystalk import -S /root/hosts.txt Import 16 hosts from hosts.txt and mark them as in scope
./celerystalk nmap Read nmap options from config.ini and fire off one nmap scan per host
./celerystalk query watch Watch until the 16 nmap tasks finish
./celerystalk scan Read service specific commands from config.ini and generate all scan tasks
./celerystalk query watch Watch until all 282 scan tasks are pulled from the queue and completed
./celerystalk report Generate this report

This only scratches the surface. celerystalk can run your subdomain recon tools, determine which subdomains are in scope, and scan all in-scope subdomains
</commercial>
